analyzeIntent(text) {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who/)) return 'query';\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close/)) return 'control';\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new/)) return 'create';\n    if (lower.match(/fill|enter|put|type|write/)) return 'fill';\n    if   if (lower.match(/beautify|enhance|improve/)) return 'beautify';\n    if (lower.match(/save|submit|next|continue/)) return 'save';\n    return 'general';\n}\n\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks/)) return 'positive';\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate/)) return 'negative';\n    return 'neutral';\n}\n\nfunction extractFormData(text, context) {\n    const result = { fields: {} };\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    // Extract company name patterns\n    if (context === 'company_name' || lower.includes('company') || lower.includes('business')) {\n        // \"my company is X\" or \"company name is X\" or \"I am from X and my company is Y\"\n        let match = text.match(/company\\s+(?:is|name\\s+is|called)\\s+[\"']?([^\"'\\.,]+)/i);\n        if (match) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\n        \n        match = text.match(/(?:we are|i am from|this is)\\s+[\"']?([^\"'\\.,]+)/i);\n        if (match && !result.fields.companyName) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\n    }\n    \n    // Extract description/about\n    if (context === 'description' || lower.includes('sell') || lower.includes('manufacture') || lower.includes('product')) {\n        let match = text.match(/(?:we\\s+)?(?:sell|manufacture|make|produce|provide)\\s+(.+)/i);\n        if (match) result.fields.description = match[1].trim();\n        \n        // Full text as description if nothing specific matched\n        if (!result.fields.description && text.length > 20) {\n            result.fields.description = text;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Extract phone numbers\n    if (context '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9',\n            'oh': '0', 'o': '0'\n        };\n        \n        let phoneText = lower;\n        for (const [word, digit] of (fallback)\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\\nimport sys\\nimport json\\n\\ndef parse_with_pdfplumber(pdf_path):\\n    import pdfplumber\\n    text = \\\"\\\"\\n    tables = []\\n    with pdfplumber.open(pdf_path) reader = PdfReader(pdf_path)\\n    text = \\\"\\\"\\n    for page in reader.pages:\\n        text += page.extract_text() or \\\"\\\"\\n    return {\\\"text\\\": text, \\\"tables\\\": [], \\\"method\\\": \\\"PyPDF2\\\"}\\n\\ndef parse_with_tika(pdf_path):\\n    from tika import parser\\n    parsed = parser.from_file(pdf_path)\\n    return {\\\"text\\\": parsed.get(\\\"content\\\", \\\"\\\"), \\\"tables\\\": [], \\\"method\\\": \\\"tika\\\"}\\n\\ndef main():\\n    if len(sys.argv) < 2:\\n        print(json.dumps({\\\"error\\\": \\\"No file path provided\\\"}))\\n        sys.exit(1)\\n    \\n    pdf_path = sys.argv[1]\\n    \\n    # Try each method\\n    methods = [\\n        (\\\"pdfplumber\\\", parse_with_pdfplumber),\\n        (\\\"PyPDF2\\\", \\\"All PDF parsers failed\\\", \\\"text\\\": \\\"\\\"}))\\n\\nif __name__ == \\\"__main__\\\":\\n    main()\\nPDFPARSER\\n\\nchmod +x \\\"$VV/backend/parse_pdf.py\\\"\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Created PDF parser script\\\"\\n\\n# Update server.cjs with PDF upload endpoint\\ncat > \\\"$VV/backend/server.cjs\\\" << 'SERVERCODE'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW BACKEND v33.5\\n * With PDF Upload + Form Processing\\n */\\n\\nconst express = require('express');\\nconst cors = require('cors');\\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\\nconst multer = require('multer');\\nconst path = require('path');\\nconst fs = }));\\napp.use(express.json());\\napp.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));\\n\\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost' });\\n\\n// File upload setup\\nconst storage = { fileSize: 50 * 1024 * 1024 } }); // 50MB limit\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// HELPERS\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who/)) return 'query';\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close/)) return 'control';\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new/)) return 'create';\\n    if (lower.match(/fill|enter|put|type|write/)) return 'fill';\\n    if (lower.match(/company|business|name|about/)) return 'form_input';\\n    if (lower.match(/phone|number|digit/)) return 'phone_input';\\n    if (lower.match(/upload|file|pdf|catalog/)) return 'upload';\\n    if (lower.match(/beautify|enhance|improve/)) return 'beautify';\\n    if (lower.match(/save|submit|next|continue/)) return 'save';\\n    return 'general';\\n}\\n\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks/)) return 'positive';\\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate/)) return 'negative';\\n    return 'neutral';\\n}\\n\\nfunction extractFormData(text, context) {\\n    const result = { fields: {} };\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    // Extract company name patterns\\n    if (context === 'company_name' || lower.includes('company') || lower.includes('business')) {\\n        // \\\"my company is X\\\" or \\\"company name is X\\\" or \\\"I am from X and my company is Y\\\"\\n        let match = text.match(/company\\\\s+(?:is|name\\\\s+is|called)\\\\s+[\\\"']?([^\\\"'\\\\.,]+)/i);\\n        if (match) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\\n        \\n        match = text.match(/(?:we are|i am from|this is)\\\\s+[\\\"']?([^\\\"'\\\\.,]+)/i);\\n        if (match && !result.fields.companyName) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract description/about\\n    if (context === 'description' || lower.includes('sell') || lower.includes('manufacture') || lower.includes('product')) {\\n        let match = text.match(/(?:we\\\\s+)?(?:sell|manufacture|make|produce|provide)\\\\s+(.+)/i);\\n        if (match) result.fields.description = match[1].trim();\\n        \\n        // Full text as description if nothing specific matched\\n        if (!result.fields.description && text.length > 20) {\\n            result.fields.description = text;\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract phone numbers\\n    if (context === 'phone' || lower.match(/\\\\d/)) {\\n        // Convert spoken numbers\\n        const numberWords = {\\n            'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\\n            'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9',\\n            'oh': '0', 'o': '0'\\n        };\\n        \\n        let phoneText = lower;\\n        for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\\n            phoneText = phoneText.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\\\\\b${word}\\\\\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Extract digits\\n        const digits = phoneText.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n        if (digits.length >= 10) {\\n            result.fields.phone = digits.slice(0, 10);\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    return result;\\n}\\n\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment, context) {\\n    const responses = {\\n        form_input: \\\"Got it! progress...\\\",\\n        upload: \\\"Processing your upload...\\\",\\n        fill: \\\"Filling in the form...\\\",\\n        navigation: \\\"Taking you there!\\\",\\n        query: \\\"Searching...\\\",\\n        control: \\\"Done!\\\",\\n        general: \\\"Got it, boss!\\\"\\n    };\\n    return responses[intent] || responses.general;\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// fields\n * Works with useVoice to fill forms from speech\n */\n\nimport { useCallback, useRef } from 'react';\n\ninterface FormFillerOptions {\n    typingSpeed?: number;  // ms per character\n    onComplete?: () => void;\n    onStart?: () => void;\n}\n\nexport function useFormFiller(options: FormFillerOptions = {}) {\n    const { typingSpeed = 30, onComplete, onStart } = options;\n    const isFillingRef = useRef(false);\n    const abortRef = useRef(false);\n    \n    /**\n     * Fill a field with typewriter animation\n     */\n    const fillField = useCallback(async (\n        element: HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | null,\n        text: string\n    ): Promise<void> => {\n        if (!element || !text) return;\n        \n        isFillingRef.current = true;\n        abortRef.current = false;\n        onStart?.();\n        \n        // Clear existing value\n        element.value = '';\n        element.focus();\n        \n        // Add filling class for styling\n        element.classList.add('vv-filling');\n        \n        // Type each character\n        for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {\n            if (abortRef.current) break;\n            \n            element.value = text.substring(0, i + 1);\n            \n            // Trigger input event for React state updates\n            const event = new Event('input', { bubbles: true });\n            element.dispatchEvent(event);\n            \n            // Also trigger change for some frameworks\n            const changeEvent = new Event('change', { bubbles: true });\n            element.dispatchEvent(changeEvent);\n            \n            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, typingSpeed));\n        }\n        \n        element.classList.remove('vv-filling');\n        element.classList.add('vv-filled');\n        \n        // Remove filled class after animation\n        setTimeout(() => element.classList.remove('vv-filled'), 1000);\n        \n        isFillingRef.current = false;\n        onComplete?.();\n    }, [typingSpeed, onComplete, onStart]);\n    \n    /**\n     * Fill multiple fields from formData\n     */\n    const fillForm = useCallback(async (\n        formData: Record<string, string>,\n        fieldMap: Record<string, string>  // { fieldName: 'selector' }\n    ): Promise<void> => {\n        for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(formData)) {\n            const selector = fieldMap[field];\n            if (!selector || !value) continue;\n            \n            const element = document.querySelector(selector) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\n            if (element) {\n                await fillField(element, value);\n                await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200)); // Pause between fields\n            }\n        }\n    }, [fillField]);\n    \n    /**\n     * Fill by field ID\n     */\n    const fillById = useCallback(async (\n        id: string,\n        text: string\n    ): Promise<void> => {\n        const element = document.getElementById(id) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\n        await fillField(element, text);\n    }, [fillField]);\n    \n    /**\n     * Fill by field name\n     */\n    const fillByName = useCallback(async (\n        name: string,\n        text: string\n    ): Promise<void> => {\n        const element = document.querySelector(`[name=\"${name}\"]`) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\n        await fillField(element, text);\n    }, [fillField]);\n    \n    /**\n     * Abort current filling\n     */\n    const abort = useCallback(() => {\n        abortRef.current = true;\n    }, []);\n    \n    return {\n        fillField,\n        fillForm,\n        fillById,\n        fillByName,\n        abort,\n        isFilling: isFillingRef.current\n    };\n}\n\nexport default useFormFiller;\nFORMFILLER\n\necho \"  \u2705 Created \\n        // Add filling class for styling\\n        element.classList.add('vv-filling');\\n        \\n        // Type each character\\n        for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {\\n event = new Event('input', { bubbles: true });\\n            element.dispatchEvent(event);\\n            \\n            // Also trigger change for some frameworks\\n            const changeEvent = new Event('change', { bubbles: true });\\n            element.dispatchEvent(changeEvent);\\n            \\n            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, typingSpeed));\\n        }\\n        \\n            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200)); // Pause between fields\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }, [fillField]);\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Fill by field ID\\n     */\\n    const \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udce4 STEP 5: Creating upload service...\"\n\nmkdir -p \"$VV/src/services\"\n\ncat > \"$VV/src/services/uploadService.ts\" << 'UPLOADSERVICE'\n/**\n * Upload Service\n * Handles    products?: Array<{ id: number; name: string; raw: string }>;\n    preview?: string;\n    error?: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * Upload PDF catalog to backend for parsing\n */\nexport async function uploadPdfCatalog(file: File): Promise<UploadResult> {\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('file', file);\n    \n    try {\n        console.log('[Upload] Sending PDF to backend:', file.name);\n        \n        const response = await fetch(API_ENDPOINTS.uploadPdf, {\n            method: 'POST',\n            body: formData\n            // Don't set Content-Type header - browser will set it with boundary\n        });\n        \n        if (!response.ok) {\n            throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`);\n        }\n        \n        const result = await response.json();\n        console.log('[Upload] Result:', result);\n        \n        return result;\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error('[Upload] Error:', error);\n        return {\n            success: false,\n            error: error.message || 'Upload failed'\n        };\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Upload any file\n */\nexport async function uploadFile(file: File, endpoint: string = API_ENDPOINTS.uploadPdf): Promise<UploadResult> {\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('file', file);\n    \n    try {\n        const response = await fetch(endpoint, {\n            method: 'POST',\n            body: formData\n        });\n        \n        return await response.json();\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        return { success: false, error: error.message };\n    }\n}\n\nexport default { uploadPdfCatalog, uploadFile };\nUPLOADSERVICE\n\necho \"  \u2705 Created
